PUBLIC NOTICES
Jagadeesh. P, a male child born to Thiru E. Pugalendran on 5th July 1993, residing at No. 2/1, Shanmuga Sundaram
Street, Muthamil Nagar, Saligramam, Chennai-600 093, Tamil Nadu, has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual
reassignment surgery by Dr. V. Jayaraman Shivan Vishua Speciality Hospital Bangalore, Karnataka by this, I may be treated
as a female and shall henceforth be known as JENILYA. P
Chennai,
13th May 2019.

JAGADEESH. P

G. Srinevasan, a male child born to Thiru Govindarajan on 2nd March 1990, residing at No. 100, 8th Street, Kamarajar
Colony, Kodambakkam, Chennai-600 024, has been living as a female, she has been granted an identity Card No. 2942/09
issued by the Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP Department, By this I, may be treated as a female
and shall henceforth be known as SADHANA. G
Chennai,
13th May 2019.

G. SRINEVASAN

R. Anand, a male child born to Thiru P. Rajamani on 9th May 1986, residing at No. 545, Ambedkar Street, Church
Compound MGR Nagar, Putlur, Thiruvallur, has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery by
Dr. Revathi. MBBS, DGO(Civil Assistant Surgeon), Government District Head Quarters Hospital, Thiruvallur-602 025, By this
I, may be treated as a female and shall henceforth be known as R. ANANTHI
Thiruvallur,
17th May 2019.

R. ANAND
